(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )

    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

The environment is a room containing various objects. Some of these objects are on, in, or contained within other objects and receptacles. You will initially be located as init_receptacle. You can assume all receptacles are freely reachable.

You arrive at bed 1. On the bed 1, you see a book 2, a book 1, a laptop 1, and a pillow 1.


Only the following actions are allowed: (There are only two types: object and receptacle)
1. go to a receptacle
    :action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
2. open a receptacle if it is closed
    :action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
3. close a receptacle
    :action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
4. take an object from another receptacle
    :action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
5. put object into/on/in another receptacle
    :action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

    :action useObject

7. heat an object using a receptacle
    :action HeatObject

8. clean an object using a receptacle
    :action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
9. cool an object using a receptacle
    :action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
10. slice an object using a sharp object
    :action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)

You must go to a receptacle first in order to use/open it or take/put objects from/on it.

The process involves two main stages:

1. Always searching for the aim Object first!!!
    In this stage, your goal is to go to and may need to open new, unvisited recepatacles until you find the object mentioned in the task. Some receptacles cannot be opened so you can directly see what objects after you go to that receptacle.

    You can only use the GotoLocation action to travel to a new location and the OpenObject action (if the receptacle is closed) to verify whether it contains the target object.

        You goal should look like this:
        (:goal 
            (at ?recepatacle)
        ) where recepatacle should be somewhere or some recepatacles not visited.

        (:goal

        ) where recepatacle should be the recepatacle you want to open.

2. After you seeing the aim object in any receptacle, using the Object to Complete the Task:

Remember your goal is Your task is to: put some pencil on shelf.. Based on different adjectives, you may need to perform different actions for the object in different ways.

    This may involve more than simply transferring it from one place to another.

    If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.
    Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

    Hint: 
    1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

    3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

    :effect (and (sliced ?co))

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)

    :effect (cleaned ?o)

1. go to a receptacle
    :action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
2. open a receptacle if it is closed
    :action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
3. close a receptacle
    :action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
4. take an object from another receptacle
    :action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
5. put object into/on/in another receptacle
    :action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

    :action HeatObject

8. clean an object using a receptacle
    :action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
9. cool an object using a receptacle
    :action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
10. slice an object using a sharp object
    :action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)

You must go to a receptacle first in order to use/open it or take/put objects from/on it.

The process involves two main stages:

1. Always searching for the aim Object first!!!
    In this stage, your goal is to go to and may need to open new, unvisited recepatacles until you find the object mentioned in the task. Some receptacles cannot be opened so you can directly see what objects after you go to that receptacle.

    You can only use the GotoLocation action to travel to a new location and the OpenObject action (if the receptacle is closed) to verify whether it contains the target object.

        You goal should look like this:

        ) where recepatacle should be somewhere or some recepatacles not visited.

    Goal 1.2: If you already go to the recepatacle and found the recepatacle is closed, use the OpenObject action to open it and inspect the contents. 
        Your goal should look like this:
        (:goal 
            (opened ?recepatacle)
        ) where recepatacle should be the recepatacle you want to open.

2. After you seeing the aim object in any receptacle, using the Object to Complete the Task:
    After you have located the object (the object may have some numbers added), you should always first pick up the object from that receptacle and update your goal to focus on how the object is used to complete the task. Remember your goal is Your task is to: put some pencil on shelf.. Based on different adjectives, you may need to perform different actions for the object in different ways.

    This may involve more than simply transferring it from one place to another.
    For example: You might examine the object or a nearby receptacle to gather information. You may need to use another tool or device (like a lamp or a switch). Some tasks require you to slice, heat, cool, or clean the object using an appropriate receptacle (e.g., microwave, sink, fridge).

    If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.
    Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

    Hint: 
    1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.
    2. If you want to slice an object, you should first go to the receptacle where both the sharp object and the aim object are located and ONLY pick up the sharp object then do the slice action. Don't forget to put the sharp object back to the receptacle after you finish slicing.
    3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
    4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem task_put_pencil_on_shelf)
  (:domain room_exploration)
  (:objects 
    init_receptacle - receptacle
    bed1 - receptacle
    cabinet4 - receptacle
    cabinet3 - receptacle
    cabinet2 - receptacle
    cabinet1 - receptacle
    desk1 - receptacle
    drawer2 - receptacle
    drawer1 - receptacle
    garbagecan1 - receptacle
    shelf1 - receptacle
    sidetable1 - receptacle
    book2 - object
    book1 - object
    laptop1 - object
    pillow1 - object
  )
  (:init 
    (at cabinet3)
    (opened bed1)
    (opened cabinet4)
    (in book2 bed1)
    (in book1 bed1)
    (in laptop1 bed1)
    (in pillow1 bed1)
    (handempty)
  )
  (:goal (opened cabinet3))
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

1. go to a receptacle
    :action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)

    :action OpenObject

    :action PickupObject

10. slice an object using a sharp object

You must go to a receptacle first in order to use/open it or take/put objects from/on it.

The process involves two main stages:

1. Always searching for the aim Object first!!!
    In this stage, your goal is to go to and may need to open new, unvisited recepatacles until you find the object mentioned in the task. Some receptacles cannot be opened so you can directly see what objects after you go to that receptacle.

    Goal 1.1: Reach a location that has not been visited (the location should be a receptacle) using the GotoLocation action. 
        You goal should look like this:

            (at ?recepatacle)
        ) where recepatacle should be somewhere or some recepatacles not visited.

    Goal 1.2: If you already go to the recepatacle and found the recepatacle is closed, use the OpenObject action to open it and inspect the contents. 
        Your goal should look like this:
        (:goal 
            (opened ?recepatacle)
        ) where recepatacle should be the recepatacle you want to open.

2. After you seeing the aim object in any receptacle, using the Object to Complete the Task:

Remember your goal is You open the cabinet 2. The cabinet 2 is open. In it, you see nothing.. Based on different adjectives, you may need to perform different actions for the object in different ways.

    This may involve more than simply transferring it from one place to another.
    For example: You might examine the object or a nearby receptacle to gather information. You may need to use another tool or device (like a lamp or a switch). Some tasks require you to slice, heat, cool, or clean the object using an appropriate receptacle (e.g., microwave, sink, fridge).

    If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.
    Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

    Hint: 
    1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.
    2. If you want to slice an object, you should first go to the receptacle where both the sharp object and the aim object are located and ONLY pick up the sharp object then do the slice action. Don't forget to put the sharp object back to the receptacle after you finish slicing.
    3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
    4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

Note: 
1. some receptacles have numbers in their names. Always keep them as they are. For example, "towelholder1" should not be changed to "towelholder".
2. Your initial goal should always be to go to a new location instead of put something into somewhere.
3. Do not enter stage 2 when not finishing stage 1.

Note: Always include :negative-preconditions in your :requirements whenever you use (not …) or delete effects, and never leave an :precondition or :effect block empty—either omit it or include at least one literal.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)

    :effect (cooled ?o)

    :effect (and (sliced ?co))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

    In this stage, your goal is to go to and may need to open new, unvisited recepatacles until you find the object mentioned in the task. Some receptacles cannot be opened so you can directly see what objects after you go to that receptacle.

    You can only use the GotoLocation action to travel to a new location and the OpenObject action (if the receptacle is closed) to verify whether it contains the target object.

    Goal 1.1: Reach a location that has not been visited (the location should be a receptacle) using the GotoLocation action. 
        You goal should look like this:
        (:goal 
            (at ?recepatacle)
        ) where recepatacle should be somewhere or some recepatacles not visited.

    Goal 1.2: If you already go to the recepatacle and found the recepatacle is closed, use the OpenObject action to open it and inspect the contents. 
        Your goal should look like this:
        (:goal 
            (opened ?recepatacle)
        ) where recepatacle should be the recepatacle you want to open.

2. After you seeing the aim object in any receptacle, using the Object to Complete the Task:
    After you have located the object (the object may have some numbers added), you should always first pick up the object from that receptacle and update your goal to focus on how the object is used to complete the task. Remember your goal is You open the cabinet 2. The cabinet 2 is open. In it, you see nothing.. Based on different adjectives, you may need to perform different actions for the object in different ways.

    This may involve more than simply transferring it from one place to another.
    For example: You might examine the object or a nearby receptacle to gather information. You may need to use another tool or device (like a lamp or a switch). Some tasks require you to slice, heat, cool, or clean the object using an appropriate receptacle (e.g., microwave, sink, fridge).

    If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.
    Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

    Hint: 
    1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.
    2. If you want to slice an object, you should first go to the receptacle where both the sharp object and the aim object are located and ONLY pick up the sharp object then do the slice action. Don't forget to put the sharp object back to the receptacle after you finish slicing.
    3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
    4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

Note: 
1. some receptacles have numbers in their names. Always keep them as they are. For example, "towelholder1" should not be changed to "towelholder".
2. Your initial goal should always be to go to a new location instead of put something into somewhere.
3. Do not enter stage 2 when not finishing stage 1.

Note: Always include :negative-preconditions in your :requirements whenever you use (not …) or delete effects, and never leave an :precondition or :effect block empty—either omit it or include at least one literal.

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    object 
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

    1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (in ?sharp_o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object - physobj
    receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject

    :effect (and (sliced ?co))
  )

(define (domain room_exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types 
    physobj
    object receptacle - physobj
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates 
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (handempty)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (visited ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to) (visited ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handempty))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (handempty)) (not (in ?o ?r)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (handempty) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (handempty)
    :effect (used ?o)
